 com / aajtak Accident is a common practice in India and deaths due to accident are hardly a major issue
 is desh main log kabhi road par to kabhi train se katkar marate rahete hai
 Now even the lives of those who lost their lives are increasing by drowning in water
 neshnal krime records beuro (NCRB) ke hal hi main jari kiye gaye aakade bhi kuch yahi kahani bayaan karte hai
 NCRB data shows that cases of discrete accidents are increasing very rapidly in India
 2014 main durghatnaon ke maamalon main 12
 The 8 per cent increase is a testimony to this fact
 kya hai kaaran?accident kya sirf sadak par hote hai? agar aap aise khyaal rakhte hai to kaaphi had tak aap galat hai
 About 4 from the accident
 5 lakh apni jaan gavante hai or unamem sabase bada kaaran road-accident ke alawa bhi kai or kaaran bhi he jinaki vajah se logon ko apni jaan gavanin pad rahi he
 Many people have lost their lives by drowning, while many have been victims of poison
 sabase bade kaaran?trephic accident aaj bhi sabase bada kaaran bana hua he
 About 37
 4 fisadi log sirf troffic accident main jaan gavaan rahe hai, matlab har paanch main do maut sirf kaa kaaran road accident he
